Yangtze River Water Freight Surcharge - Shipping Industry Requests Reduction 123

Concrete Measures Not Yet Decided at Yesterday's Meeting

The Shanghai Shipping Association states that since the six shipping companies, including Jardine Matheson, Swire, China Merchants, Nissin, Sanbei, and Ning Shao, jointly implemented a water freight surcharge for the Yangtze River route, cargo transportation has been measured using a standardized company scale, resulting in a doubling of water freight costs. The Shanghai Customs Brokers Association and the Foreign General Merchandise Customs Brokers, considering the current period of commercial decline and the difficulty of maintaining existing water freight rates, sent representatives to request a reduction in water freight from the companies to sustain their business. To date, no progress has been made. Yesterday at 2 PM, the six companies held a meeting at the Shipping Club. Representatives from the Shanghai Customs Brokerage industry, including Association Chairman Chen Pan Shi, and foreign general merchandise customs brokers Cao Fuyuan, Yang Zhiqing, and Dai Chen, attended the meeting. Chairman Zhi Mu from Swire was appointed to preside. The customs broker representatives presented their requests, outlining their difficulties and hoping for a reduction in water freight rates on the Yangtze River route to sustain their businesses and alleviate the suffering of merchants. However, after discussions, no concrete measures were decided upon, and the issue will be submitted for a decision at the next meeting.

China International Famine Relief Commission - Relief for Disease-Stricken Victims in Western Shandong 124

There are still four to five hundred thousand people living without food or shelter, and the spring cold in the disaster area is severe. Although daytime temperatures reach around ten degrees Fahrenheit, they drop below freezing at night. Floods cover the land with ice, and the disaster victims live in an ice world. Furthermore, tree bark and grass roots have been exhausted. They have no place to live and no food to eat. The disaster victims are dying from starvation or freezing. Moreover, eight or nine out of ten are suffering from measles, smallpox, skin diseases, and other infectious diseases. The commission has established dozens of temporary disaster relief hospitals in Jinan, Jining, Yanzhou, Longshan, Teng County, Juye County, Wenshang, Tai'an, Fei County, Cao County, and other places. Each hospital diagnoses over a hundred people daily. Even at Qilu Hospital alone, approximately nine thousand people received medical treatment and vaccinations at various shelters in December of last year. It is evident that in addition to suffering from cold and hunger, disease is a serious problem facing the disaster victims in western Shandong. Philanthropists should find ways to save them.

Lu Bohong Discusses the Dire Situation of Drought and Flooding in Luxu 125

Philanthropist Lu Bohong was sent by the fundraising committees of various provinces to inspect the drought and flood conditions in Xuzhou, Shandong, and Bengbu last month. He returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday. According to him, the floodwaters in the affected areas of Shandong have not receded, and over a hundred thousand disaster victims are trapped without food or clothing, which is a dire situation. Even the shelters and temporary hospitals in Jinan are still accommodating tens of thousands of homeless disaster victims. Chairman Han is deeply concerned and has agreed to cooperate with the flood relief committees to provide assistance. After holding a spring relief meeting, it was decided that the urgent tasks are: 1. Purchasing food for March and April; 2. Purchasing plowing cattle and farm tools; 3. Repairing houses damaged by the floods; 4. Purchasing spring planting seeds, etc. The situation in Xuzhou and the proposed measures are generally similar to those in Shandong, but the disaster area is not as extensive. He then went to Bengbu and met with Father Disder of the Catholic Church and local gentry to discuss the severe drought conditions, which are no less severe than the floods in Xuzhou and Shandong, particularly in the four counties of Huo Qiu, Meng County, Ying Shang, and Fuyang. In summary, the disasters in all these places are severe and widespread. Effective relief efforts require at least one million yuan. He has sent letters to the flood relief fundraising committees and the international famine relief committees to seek assistance.

Gu A'quan and Yao Wenhan - Selling Pornographic Pictures, Both Chinese and Western Styles 129

A Business that Corrupts Morals - Each Sentenced to a Fine of 500 Yuan

Lu Dagong, the Chinese head of the Lao Zha Public Concession, and Chinese detective Lang Chengpei, inspected various hotels at 10:45 PM on the 29th of last month. When they inspected room 27 of the Tongli Public Hotel at 195 Fujian Road, they found Gu A'quan from Shanghai and Yao Wenhan from Suzhou living there. After a search by the head, a large number of pornographic pictures were found in a rattan suitcase. The pictures included both Chinese and Western styles, totaling hundreds of pieces. It was indeed an organization selling pornographic pictures. Therefore, Gu and Yao were taken back to the police station and handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday, Judge Yang Qianchang reopened the criminal court for further questioning. Lawyer Jiang Baolian from the police station prosecuted them for violating public morals. Then, the head and others reported the process of the investigation. According to Gu, the pictures were deposited by a friend. Yao stated that although he had been engaged in this business before, he had reformed after being caught and punished. He had just sat down at the hotel when he was arrested. Judge Yang believed that the defendants could engage in any business, but they engaged in this business that corrupted morals and harmed young people. Unless they were severely punished, it would not be enough to deter others. Therefore, he announced the judgment, fining Gu and Yao 500 yuan each. If they chose to perform labor, it would be at a rate of three yuan per day. The pornographic pictures were confiscated.

Reasons for the Soaring Price of Soybean Oil 130

In reality, it is being manipulated by a certain party. Shanghai Oil Factories are trying to find a way to save the situation.

The Central News Agency reports that soybean oil has a very wide market in China. Its main sources are Dalian, Yingkou, Niuzhuang, and other places. The three northeastern provinces are particularly rich in soybeans. In addition to transporting soybeans to various ports for sale, they are also pressed into soybean oil and sold in the interior. However, since the Northeast was occupied, all kinds of production have been manipulated, and soybean oil is inevitably monopolized. Therefore, the price of soybean oil has been soaring recently. It is understood that in the past, a large number of soybeans and soybean oil were transported from the Northeast to Shanghai. However, since last year, the soybeans produced in various parts of the Northeast have been manipulated by a certain party, and the production of soybean oil has become increasingly scarce, which has led to the soaring price of soybean oil in the country. The highest price reached 20 yuan per picul, which is 5 or 6 yuan higher than in the past. The Shanghai oil factories are running out of raw materials from the Northeast, and the domestic production is minimal, so there is no way to meet the market demand. The oil factories are now planning to find ways to save the situation, such as replacing it with rapeseed oil and raw oil. Rapeseed and peanuts are still abundant and cheap in China. If they can be used, they can both resist the manipulation of the soybean market by a certain party and meet the needs of the market.

Raw Silk and Finished Silk Industries - A Portion of the Public Assessment Has Been Decided 135

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Shanghai Raw Silk Association, since being ordered by the ministry to switch to using the municipal public foot (unit of measurement) for pricing, has been well-received by customers due to its convenience in calculation. However, at the end of February when settling accounts, customers still felt the pricing was too high. Therefore, the Silk and Satin Industry Association and the Electric Silk Weaving Factory Association, together with their affiliated associations (Zhejiang Provincial Association, Qianjiang Guild Hall, Yunjin Guild Hall, Shengjing Guild Hall, etc.), came forward to request that the Fine Weaving Association reduce the public assessment price per foot. After several meetings, the pricing for the Zhejiang Raw Silk Association's silk has been announced as follows: 3.5 fen per foot for top-grade, 3 fen for medium-grade, 2.5 fen for light-grade, and 2 fen for the lightest-grade. The Electric Silk Weaving Factory Association has also decided on a pricing of 2.5 fen per foot for grade A genuine silk/artificial silk woven goods, 2 fen for grade B, and 1.5 fen for grade C. However, the pricing for the Silk and Satin Industry Association is still under discussion. As the public assessments are being changed one after another, the fine weaving factories have no choice but to reorganize their accounts, which has been very busy in recent days. It can be said that the two industries have spared no effort to promote its success, and can be described as wiping clean for a fresh start.

Detective Tao Shiwei of the Xin Zha Police Station Uncovers the X-Ray Mirror - Under the Guise of Science, it Truly Exhibits Immorality - The Beautiful Woman Turns into a Skeleton - A Detestable Third Act 136

In general entertainment venues in Shanghai, in order to attract customers recently, in addition to various entertainment activities, they have mostly added an X-ray mirror section, saying that it uses scientific methods to see through the body and turn it into a skeleton, attracting many curious people to be tempted. Everyone wants to see it first, and the venue owner stipulates that the cost of visiting is two cents per person. In reality, the so-called scientific change is purely a deception. The other day, Detective Tao Shiwei of the Xin Zha Police Station, while inspecting the Shanghai World Entertainment Venue on Jing'an Temple Road, made a special visit to the X-ray section and carefully observed it, immediately exposing this dark secret of teaching licentiousness and defrauding money. The so-called X-ray mirror is placed in a dark room. When someone enters to view it, the manager turns on the light on one side and orders a young woman to stand behind the mirror in a yukata (bathing gown), and her graceful shadow is revealed from the mirror. This is the phenomenon of the first act. Then, the manager turns the light from bright to dark, and then immediately restores the light. In this moment, the person standing behind the mirror has been replaced by someone else, and the clothes have also been changed to only wearing a shirt and pants. However, the former faced the mirror, while this one faces the wall, so the mirror shows the back of the beautiful woman's neck, and it is impossible to see her true face. This is the change of the second act. At this time, the manager still uses the same trick, turning the light off and then on again, so that the person behind the mirror retreats and is replaced by the girl who appeared in the first act, but she is completely naked, with every detail visible. Therefore, both the performers and the audience recognize that this third act is the most exciting, but it harms public morals, especially in this act. When the audience is focused, the fourth act is performed. What appears in the mirror is a skeleton. This object is man-made, and the so-called "beautiful woman turns into a skeleton" is also the end of the viewing. However, the customers still have regrets about the fleeting glimpse of the third act, so they often shout the slogan "One more time!" Whenever the manager sees the enthusiastic requests from the audience, he orders the performing girl to sacrifice her sex appeal and repeat the act, so that the viewers can feast their eyes. Detective Tao, having discovered this secret that day, recognized the need to immediately crack down on it. In addition to joining forces with foreign detective Huierkaosi to go to the venue to order that the performance be prohibited, he also found out that among the two women who performed, the naked one was named Shi Fengying, who is 22 years old. He immediately brought her, along with the venue manager Hu Chao (named Fengxiang), to public prosecution. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang of the First Special District Court summoned them for questioning. Lawyer Jiang Baolian of the police station presented the course of events. Judge Yang stated that Shi Fengying had not yet been summoned, and after briefly questioning Hu, he ordered him to pay a 1,000 yuan deposit and adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Tobacco Exchange Industry Notice to Fellow Businesses - Pay Attention to Three Inspections - Tax Evasion, Stamps, and Weights and Measures 144

The Shanghai South Office of the Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Industry Association, in view of the fact that most of its members are small businesses and women's stores with limited business knowledge, and therefore most of the goods they sell are brought to their doors by street vendors, often being deceived and fined for detention by the tax bureau, issued an emergency notice yesterday to protect its members from being penalized, saying, "Informing you, in recent times, various agencies have been rigorously inspecting and penalizing counterfeit goods and tax evasion. We hereby notify you so that everyone is aware. The key points of the inspection include the following three items, which are listed in detail below: Recently, several cases have been discovered of various counterfeit brand matches, cigarettes, and cigars being sold door-to-door and seized and penalized by the tax bureau. All our members should pay attention and refuse to sell goods sold door-to-door to avoid being deceived, implicated, and penalized. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau will soon send uniformed police officers to conduct a spring inspection of stamp tax. The ledgers, account books, and all other contracts and evidence used by member stores should be fully stamped according to the new regulations, and the stamps must be covered with a overlapping seal to avoid omissions or short stamps, which will result in fines. The Municipal Social Bureau's Bureau of Weights and Measures will soon conduct a general inspection. All member stores should pay attention to purchasing weights and measures (scales, rulers, bushels, pecks, hanging scales, etc.) that have been inspected by the bureau and stamped with a hard stamp. The use of any uninspected items is prohibited. If discovered, you will be summoned and fined by the court. Please pay attention to the above three items and do not neglect them to your own detriment. This is an important notice."

Maritime Bureau Ship Collision Meeting - Public Judgment of Disputes - Public Judgment Results Separately Notified to Each Company - Xin Jiangtian Case Has Been Submitted to the Ministry for Instructions 145

The Shanghai Maritime Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation's Ship Collision Dispute Committee held its twenty-first decision meeting at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 5th. Committee members Chen Ganqing, Shen Jiyun, Chen Baoyan, and He Daoyu attended, with Hu Hanwu and Shi Jisheng present. Ship captains and chief mates of various transport companies, including Long Xianglin, Tang Youxi, Pu Yigou, helmsman Shi Caicai, and Yuan Kezheng of the Yuanli Salt Ship, etc., were present. The meeting was chaired by Peng Hu, Director of the Shanghai Maritime Bureau, with Hu Hanwu as the recorder. The following cases were publicly judged: Case of the Yongyu Shipping Company's Dalian transport colliding with the Salt Inspectorate's Jixi vessel in front of the Jianghai Customs on January 31. It was decided that the Jixi vessel should bear 60% of the responsibility for the negligence, and the Dalian transport should bear 40% of the responsibility. Case of the Yongyu Shipping Company's Dalian transport colliding with the Yongyuan tugboat No. 1, towed by Taichang Shipping Bureau, near Lujiazui. It was decided that the Yongyuan tugboat should bear full responsibility for the negligence in this case. Case of the Ruian Company's Xinruian colliding with the Yuanli salt ship in the Huangpu River. It was decided that the Xinruian vessel should bear 50% of the responsibility for the negligence, and the Yuanli salt ship should bear 50% of the responsibility. As for the case of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Jiangtian sinking a sailboat, due to its importance, the Maritime Bureau has submitted the findings of the investigation from all parties, as well as the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's reply, the list of losses of the sailboat, and the number of crew deaths, to the Ministry for instructions. This will be submitted for public judgment after the Ministry's approval.

The winning lottery tickets can be cashed at the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various places one week later. The validity period is from March 14 to August 30, 1936. During the lottery, the lottery office specially contracted China News Agency, Buddhist Sounds, Huamei, Wonderful News, and Jianhua Radio Stations to broadcast the winning numbers in Chinese, American, Russian, and French. The twenty-first issue of lottery tickets will start today and will be drawn on April 3.

Fenjiu Industry Association Opposes Increasing Stand Donations 149

Yesterday, a letter was sent to the French Concession Taxpayer Association requesting them to negotiate with the French Municipal Council to abolish the tax.

The Fenjiu Industry Association of this city believes that the sudden increase in stall taxes by the French Concession Council hinders commercial development. Yesterday, it sent a letter to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayer Association, requesting them to negotiate and request the abolition of stall taxes in order to maintain the industry's livelihood. The original letter stated, "To whom it may concern, according to the reports from our members Xinsheng Wine Shop, Renji Kanghou Wine Shop, Dade Wine Shop, etc., regarding the application, our members have been operating in the French Concession for many years. Now that the market is depressed and business losses are very large, it is difficult to maintain. Suddenly, we received a letter from the Taxation Department of the French Concession Council stating that, starting in February of the lunar calendar, each household must pay an additional third of the stall tax. Our members directly negotiated to no avail and had no choice but to request the general assembly to transfer the negotiation in order to reduce the burden and maintain business. The situation is extremely urgent, etc., to the association. Based on this, it has been found that the market is depressed, and all industries are sluggish. Our members are generally small-scale businesses and are already difficult to maintain at ordinary times. How can we add additional donations to increase the burden? This is the real situation. This matter concerns the issue of Chinese taxpayers. In addition to our association directly asking the French Concession Council to exempt the increase, we should ask your association to provide strong support for the citizens in the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation and negotiate on our behalf to avoid the increase. Our members will be truly grateful. A corresponding letter is sent to your association, hoping that you will check and inform us of the handling situation. After receiving this request, the association sent staff to the Fenjiu Industry Association and various Fenjiu shops to conduct on-site investigations on the business situation and tax rates of the Fenjiu industry, etc., in order to have a basis for submitting a negotiation to the French Concession Council, requesting its abolition."

Zhuanqiao People's Education Center Improves Funerals 153

The Zhuanqiao People's Education Center in Shanghai County has formulated five preliminary measures for improving folk funerals and submitted them to the county for record and implementation: Friends and relatives should use legal tender for gifts, without purchasing incense, bracelets, silver ingots, silk, etc. As a principle, burning clothes when dying should be avoided. If you want to burn them, only those that the patient took when sick are allowed. The banquet for the bereaved family should be limited to three seats for the initial funeral and no more than eight seats for the funeral. The body must be placed in the coffin within thirty-six hours of death, and the coffin must be buried within six months. The burial of each coffin should not exceed fifty square feet, and flowers and trees must be planted in the cemetery.

Municipal Health Bureau Bans "Bing She" Within the City 155

Complete Relocation by the End of June This Year, No New Construction Allowed for Unrelocated "Bing She"

The Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the fact that the "bing she" (a type of lodging house, often for people from the same hometown) belonging to various hometown associations within the territory are mostly located in densely populated areas, which is detrimental to hygiene, ordered in the spring of the 23rd year of the Republic to relocate them within designated areas in order to prioritize hygiene. As the deadline is approaching, the bureau has issued another order urging relocation. The document states: "In order to supervise and urge compliance with the timely relocation of 'bing she' outside the designated 'bing she' area in this city, the municipal government has ordered that another announcement be made. The rules for banning 'bing she' on schedule set the end of June of the 25th year as the final deadline. By the deadline, all existing 'bing she' in this city must be appropriately located in the designated 'bing she' area. All 'bing she' in this city that have not yet been relocated to the designated area will not be allowed to build any new houses. If existing 'bing she' need to repair old houses, they must first be approved by the Engineering and Health Bureaus through joint inspection. Violators will be ordered to demolish by the Public Security Bureau. When constructing 'bing she' within the designated 'bing she' area, the Land Bureau may assist in purchasing land, etc." In addition to separate orders, this order is for compliance.

Scope of General Inspection of County Opium Addicts 161

County Government Convened Heads of Baojia to Disseminate Information by District

The general inspection of opium addicts in Shanghai County has been implemented since the 16th of this month. The county government yesterday instructed all public security bureaus, district offices, and commissioners stationed in each district to comply with the scope of the general inspection: (1) Manufacturing, selling, and using drugs. (2) Selling opium and privately smoking without a license. (3) Intending to profit by providing premises for people to smoke opium or drugs, or using limited-term smoking cessation licenses to provide for people to smoke and implement compulsory smoking cessation, or re-smoking and stealing after abstinence, and helping to sell and smoke, and administering morphine to others are all included. In order to supervise the effective implementation of these measures, the county government yesterday ordered each district to convene the heads of townships and baojia to disseminate all information. Members from the county government and the anti-opium association will attend the meeting to provide guidance. The convening dates are: 10 AM on the 7th for the Third District, 2 PM on the 7th for the First District, 10 AM on the 9th for the Second District, 10 AM on the 10th for the Fifth District, and 2 PM on the 10th for the Fourth District.

Yao Ting Chun's Invention of a Three-Purpose Activity Name Card Holder 166

Industry Ministry Patent Applied for Ten Years

Mr. Yao Ting Chun of the press, in view of the frequent social interactions and communication with relatives and friends in daily life, which can easily lead to omissions, and the simple and vulgar content of various diaries and memos on the market, which are not practical, Yao spent more than two years of effort and a huge amount of money to invent a new three-purpose activity name message film diary book wallet. The cover of the clip is made of rose red super-grade rolled flower pattern leather, with gold-stamped trademarks. The clip is equipped with many small clips and folding pockets, and a wide and tight band in the middle that can be freely installed and removed, a gold-edged diary book, and two pages of small name message films nailed in the book, which can be turned over and used for two purposes on one film, which is very ingenious and convenient. It can hold more than one hundred names of relatives and friends. The above diary book is linked to an activity banknote clip at the back. The clip can automatically clip banknotes, and will not fall off when turned over. The clip has a transparent paper sleeve shell, which can hold various licenses, cards, and other items. It has three uses in one, is exquisite and gorgeous, strong and convenient. Because Yao intends to popularize it in society, he does not seek huge profits and sets a low price. The invention of this thing is really a daily necessity for people in society. It has been repeatedly adopted and ordered in large quantities by various major institutions such as the Ministry of Communications, the Telegraph Bureau, the International Radio Station, the Wireless Radio Station, the International Telecommunications Bureau, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau of this port, and they are very satisfied. The name message film guide recording company is now located at No. 64 Guangdong Road, telephone number 15819. It is heard that Yao's newly invented three-purpose activity name message film diary book wallet has been submitted to the Ministry of Industry, requesting a patent for ten years, and has extended Zhang Qing Yue lawyer as a perennial legal consultant. In the future, others must not imitate it in the same way, so as not to fall into the legal net.

The Municipal Council Orchestra to Hold Symphony Concert Tomorrow

The Municipal Council Orchestra will hold its 22nd weekly music concert as usual at 5:15 PM tomorrow (Sunday) at the Lyceum Theatre in the French Concession. The program that day will be of a symphonic nature. The most interesting piece is the second part of Strauss's large-scale "Bourgeois Gentleman". It is said that this piece is not often performed even in major European and American cities, so it is a rare opportunity in this port. In addition, there will be solo performances on the violin, cello, and piano.

Unidentified Male Corpse on Xietu Road. An unidentified male corpse was found yesterday morning on the side of the road west of Jinyi Bridge Road, Xietu Road, Shanghai West. He was wearing blue cloth shirt and trousers, about 30 years old, and looked like a worker. The local Baodi Cao Zhongqing reported the case to the court. At 4 PM, Zhang Prosecutor and the inspector arrived at the scene for inspection. It was determined that he had died of illness. As no relatives of the deceased were found, the order was given to the Baodi to prepare a coffin, collect the body, and temporarily enshrine it for relatives to claim.

The Xujiahui Observatory’s weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and Northeast China will be clear and cold, gradually changing with strong, unstable winds, and sandstorms. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River will be cold, turning from cloudy to overcast with localized fog and variable winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and this area will have winds varying from north to east. The East China Sea and Taiwan will be cloudy with rain and strong winter monsoons. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this port was a maximum of 41.9 and a minimum of 25.5. On the same day last year, the maximum was 64.6 and the minimum was 36.5.

China and Portugal Compete for the International Cup Today; Portugal Strengthened with the Service of Le Métayer; China Team Assembled from the Elite of Two Teams, Optimism Not Warranted 178

The Chinese and Portuguese football teams will compete in the final at Yiyuan at 3 PM this afternoon to decide this year's Shanghai International Cup football championship. This is Shanghai's largest and most eye-catching championship.

The Chinese football team has won the championship three times in a row in 1930, 1931, and 1935. The Portuguese team has also won the championship before, but has not realized its desire to win the cup in recent sessions. This season, the team is very strong, so there will definitely be a fierce competition and a fascinating game.

Previously, due to a minor dispute, Marseille and Le Métayer, two inter-city players, were excluded from the Portuguese team. Now, due to various difficulties, they have been re-invited to join the Portuguese team. However, only Le Métayer will be seen in today's game. Marseille injured his knee in the charity cup game against the Chinese team and has not recovered, and is still under medical treatment.

The injury of Portuguese center Corazza has already caused Portugal to forfeit the Scota Cup. Whether he can play today is still uncertain. However, in any case, the team is a dangerous factor for the Chinese team. The Chinese team is composed of the elite of the Tung Wah and Youlian teams. Although the call for victory is very high, an unexpected result is not difficult to occur. The Chinese team members will do their best to keep the International Cup in China.

Western Youth Volleyball: Hai Qing Holds Top Position; Four Wins in Four Games; Straight Three Sets Defeat of Western Youth Last Night; Six Games in Total in Groups One and Two of Group B Today 182

The final week of the first round of the eighth Western Youth Volleyball League took place last night. Because the China Youth team withdrew, the game between that team and Mai Ling was canceled. Therefore, there was only one game last night, between Hai Qing and Western Youth. It was expected that Western Youth's skills were mediocre and could not withstand a single blow from Hai Qing. Last night, except for the second game, where Western Youth was able to rally slightly, the other two games saw Hai Qing's imposing manner and became one-sided. As a result, 15-4, 15-9, and 15-1, Hai Qing won a straight three sets and Western Youth suffered a major defeat. Hai Qing won four games in four and holds the top spot in the first round. The second round is scheduled to begin on the 9th of this month. The details of last night's game and today's schedule are listed below:

Hai Qing Takes the Lead

At 7:30, the two Western Youth teams began contact. Hai Qing served first and immediately scored one point. Zheng Mai quickly smashed the ball, taking a遥遙 lead of 6-0. Seeing that the situation was not good, Western Youth actively resisted. Burton made a leaping shot and regained one point. Hai Qing’s Grey responded in kind. Zheng Mai made several out-of-bounds shots, and Western Youth sat and won two cities. After 9-4, Hai Qing's momentum greatly increased, and they played smoothly. Western Youth had no resistance, and Hai Qing won the first game with 15-4.

Fierce Smashes

In the second game, Western Youth vowed to avenge their previous defeat.

They fought cautiously, and after several exchanges, they took the lead with a score of 3-0. Hai Qing's Zhang Renming served and scored one point. Then, Western Youth's Burton made a series of brilliant shots, and Rankin's lining was sonorous and colorful, and the score quickly became 6-2. Hai Qing's Zheng Yiquan made a leaping smash, and Mai Bingyao dived to save the ball, making it a tie. After that, each team increased their score, and they were deadlocked. At 10-9, Hai Qing suddenly added five points and won the second game with 15-9.

Western Youth Suffers a Major Defeat

At the beginning of the third game, Hai Qing took advantage of the momentum of victory and scored five points immediately. On the other hand, Western Youth had a chaotic lineup and no fighting spirit. Mai Bingyao hit the ball out of bounds, gaining a city for them. After that, Western Youth was completely defeated and had no resistance, allowing Hai Qing's artillery fire to ravage them. Hai Qing became more and more courageous, and the four Chinese generals showed their skills, and the score soared. Finally, they defeated Western Youth by a straight three sets with a score of 15-1.

China Youth Basketball League: Girls' Team Qixiu Defeats Moore; Luti Wins Against Chenguang; School Group Tax Academy Defeats Gezhi; Banking Group Guohuo Defeats Central, Winning the Championship 185

The 19th week of the China Youth Basketball League took place at the China Youth Gymnasium yesterday afternoon, with a total of five games. Two of them were in the girls' group, which opened last night. The first game was between the school group McLaren and Zhongfa. McLaren has made great progress in their skills since defeating the Tax Academy last week. Although Zhongfa is strong, it was not their opponent and lost to McLaren with a score of 30-24. The other game was between the Tax Academy and Gezhi. The Tax Academy defeated Gezhi with a score of 35-19. Then came the opening game of the girls' group between Qixiu and Moore. Qixiu is one of the best, while Moore is a rising new force. The game was tense and full of excitement. As a result, Qixiu defeated Moore with a score of 21-18. Another game was between Luti and Chenguang. Luti has strong players such as He Miaoying and Zhang Minzhi. Chenguang is a newcomer, so naturally they were no match. As a result, Luti defeated Chenguang with a score of 29-14. The last game was between the banking group Guohuo and Central. Guohuo has strong players such as Jia Youliang, Qu Xilin, and Xu Jusheng. They have already achieved a record of five wins in five games. Central is led by Cao Tingzan and Gu Shangdong. Therefore, the two sides were evenly matched. In the first half, Guohuo defeated Central with a score of 22-18. In the second half, Central tried hard to resist, but Guohuo's defense was tight, and they lost again with a score of 14-12. As a result, Guohuo won with a score of 36-28 and won the championship of the banking group.

Ministry of Education Circular: Increase Funding for Volunteer and Vocational Education; Report to the Ministry Before May 15; The Central Government Will Allocate Subsidies 189

(Nanjing, 6th) The Ministry of Education issued a circular to all education departments on the 6th, stating that volunteer and vocational education should be regarded as the central work for the next year, and the following items should be followed when preparing the budget for the 25th year:

Increase funding for volunteer education, aiming to increase it by more than double compared to the previous year. In the future, the continued allocation and increased allocation of central subsidies will be proportional to the actual amount of funding expansion for this cause in each province.

Increase funding for vocational education, striving to expand it according to the ratio of the previous year, so as to reach the proportion of vocational education funding within the time limit. Provincial governments should also be consulted to seek implementation. Each department must draft an implementation plan and list the exact amount of increased funding and report it to the Ministry for review before May 15.

(Nanjing, 6th) The central government approved a subsidy of 2.4 million yuan for compulsory education funding in the previous year, plus 500,000 yuan for border education funding and 300,000 yuan for subsidies from the Gengkuan (Boxer Indemnity) organization, totaling 3.2 million yuan. The Ministry of Education distributed the funds to various provinces and cities. Due to the establishment of volunteer schools, the cost was huge, and local fiscal revenue was limited. It is requested that the funding be increased appropriately starting from the next year. Recently, the Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect vocational and volunteer education and deeply felt the lack of funding. It has again ordered the central government to increase the subsidy for the next year in order to promote it. As for the volunteer education plans of various provinces and cities, the Ministry has ordered the provincial and municipal governments to prepare them and submit them to the Ministry for review.

Ministry of Education Discusses Middle School Curriculum Subjects 190

(Nanjing, 6th) The Ministry of Education stated that the middle school curriculum standards have been revised, and all subjects and teaching materials therein have been changed. On the 6th, experts from various subjects were specially convened in groups to discuss the matter in the morning and afternoon. The result was to reduce the number of general subjects and increase the number of special applied teaching materials.

March 15th Is the Scout Memorial Day; The Scout Association Orders Celebrations in Various Places 191

(Nanjing, 6th) The China Scout Association stated that since March 15, 1926, when the Central Committee resolved that our country's scout cause would be led by our Party and determined its organizational system, it has been nearly ten years. Therefore, this day is truly the day of the development of a new life for the scout cause. It has been stipulated that March 15th of each year is the Memorial Day for Scouts in our country. All parts of the country should hold enthusiastic celebration ceremonies to show their commemoration. Special memorial methods and celebration ceremonies have been drafted and issued to the scout councils of various provinces and cities for compliance.

National Children's Painting Exhibition Sets Standards for Entries and Judging, and Passes the List of Sponsors and Judging Committee Members; Ma Li Craft Factory Generously Donates More Than 1,000 Yuan 193

The National Children's Painting Exhibition held its fourth preparatory meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association. Attendees included Pan Gongzhan (representing Hu Shuyi), Hu Shuyi, Yan Kechang, Sun Yongyi, Qian Fugong, Ma Gongyu, Zhou Wanghe, Chen Zhengfan, Chen Tiesheng (representing Chen), and Qian Honglie attended. The details are as follows:

Important Resolutions: Chairman Pan Gongzhan (representing Hu) and Recorder Qian Honglie. First, the chairman reported that the Ma Li Craft Factory is enthusiastic about children's causes and has taken the initiative to send a letter of sponsorship, stating that they are willing to donate 200 yuan in membership fees, 500 yuan in cash prizes, and 500 yuan in in-kind prizes, etc. Then, the following matters were discussed:

Revised and passed the entry review standards.

Revised and passed the entry judging standards.

Revised and passed the reward methods.

Revised and passed the methods for children to participate in painting performances.

Passed the list of judging committee members.

Passed the list of sponsors.

Requested the National Children's Year Implementation Committee to revise the entry details, and that junior high school students under the age of fifteen may also participate in the works.

The General Affairs and Judging Committees will compile the association's handbook.

Hu Shuyi, Chen Heqin, and Ding Shujing were appointed to represent the association in Beijing to contact the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Industry, and other departments to discuss funding.

Solicit prizes to be handled by the General Affairs Department.

Entry Review Standards: National Children's Painting Exhibition Entry Review Standards: Article 1: The entries of this association shall be reviewed and passed by this association in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the Entry Solicitation Details before being selected. Article 2: The entry review standards are divided into content and technology, but must be reviewed according to children's psychology. Any works not created by the children themselves will not be selected. A. Content: Has creativity. B. Technology: Image, color, composition. Article 3: The method of review is to divide the entries into eight groups: "brush painting," "crayon painting," "pencil painting," "chalk painting," "watercolor painting," "charcoal painting," "pattern painting," and "other," and review them in groups. Article 4: The review is divided into two steps: preliminary selection and re-selection. After the preliminary selection of all entries according to the above standards, a re-selection will be held. Only entries selected for the re-selection may be displayed. Article 5: The review work will be carried out by the Judging Department of the Association in conjunction with the Judging Committee.

Judging Standards: National Children's Painting Exhibition Judging Standards: Article 1: The merits of the entries of this association shall be determined by the Judging Committee. Article 2: Judging shall be carried out in two steps: group judging and joint judging. Article 3: The judging standards are divided into content and technology, but must be judged according to children's psychology. A. Content: Has creativity. B. Technology: Image, color, composition. Article 4: The method of judging is to divide the entries into eight groups: "brush painting," "crayon painting," "pencil painting," "chalk painting," "watercolor painting," "charcoal painting," "pattern painting," and "other." Each group is further divided into five levels according to the age of the children: 4 to 6 years old is the first level, 7 to 8 years old is the second level, 9 to 10 years old is the third level, 11 to 12 years old is the fourth level, and 13 to 15 years old is the fifth level. Article 5: According to the above "standards," "groups," and "levels," scores are calculated using percentages. The ratios of content and technology are specified by level as follows: (A) Content: Level 1: 70%, Level 2: 65%, Level 3: 60%, Level 4: 55%, Level 5: 50%. (B) Technology: Level 1: 30%, Level 2: 35%, Level 3: 40%, Level 4: 45%, Level 5: 50%. Article 6: Group judging will begin on the first day after the closing ceremony. Joint judging will be carried out after the group judging is completed. Article 7: The results of the entries will be judged according to the normal distribution method. Article 8: The awarding of prizes will be officially announced after the closing ceremony of this association. Article 9: The judging report will be officially announced after the judging is completed.

Reward Methods: National Children's Painting Exhibition Reward Methods: Entries of this association will be rated according to the normal distribution method, and those listed in the first and second classes will be rewarded according to these methods. Entries of this association that are rated in the first class will be given a first-class prize, and those listed in the second class will be given a second-class prize. Schools with excellent results will be given certificates of merit by this association. Those with particularly excellent results will be presented by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee to the Ministry of Education for commendation. In addition to the foregoing methods, they may be published in a special publication of this association. Schools and individual children whose entries are selected will be given souvenirs by this association. Organizations and individuals may also set up prizes, but the reward methods must be determined and allocated by this association.

Children's Education Novel

Little Men (Part 1, 9, 2) 199

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"I must be careful; but everyone eats so much, I think I’ll just do my best." said Teddy, still inclined to that common notion that Thanksgiving is about eating almost to the point of stroke, or at least a stomachache or headache.

Everyone had been sitting for a long time, and at the end, they each toasted each other's health with apple cider, then stood up and dispersed. Mrs. Brooke then said to them, "Now, my darlings, you may play quietly, because there will be a big celebration tonight."

Mr. Brooke said, "I want to take my whole team for a ride in the carriage; that would be very enjoyable. You can rest at home, dear, or you'll be too tired tonight." After they put on their coats and hats, filled a large carriage to the brim, they immediately set off for a long and pleasant excursion, leaving Mrs. Brooke at home to rest and quietly do a few small things.

Resulting in a One Yuan Drop

Piece Goods: Flannel Shortage and Soaring Prices 209

Today, customers in various ports need to purchase flannel, and the price has soared by more than six or seven jiao per yard. Because not much new flannel has arrived in Shanghai, and the existing inventory has declined, the market is unusually lacking in goods. And when the sellers see that sales are quite strong, they all shout higher prices. Especially the grade between four yuan and five yuan is particularly brisk. Those in the industry and Western clothing tailors with sharp eyes are mostly secretly searching and absorbing, anticipating that the summer weather will turn hot, and this goods will surely become even more expensive. Currently, white and gray plain flannels are mostly considered rare goods.

Yesterday was the deadline for bidding and exchange for the Sugar Industry Cooperative. A total of 3,750 bags of Five Sheep coarse white sugar were at 22.1 yuan, up five cents, with 350 bags sold. In addition, the first batch of Quxi factory's coarse white sugar was 3,300 bags, with the quality being relatively poor. The price was two dimes lower, at 21.9 yuan, with 1,000 bags sold. No. 2 Five Sheep cotton white sugar was 88 bags at 21.1 yuan, and No. 4 was another 10 bags at 20.9 yuan, with no changes.

Metals: U.S. Company Firmly Sells 300 Tons of Iron 216

Recently, the inventory of U.S. Company iron (200 pounds per box) in the market has been thin. Yesterday, certain foreign firms, including British firms, sold 300 tons at a price of 7 gold yuan per box (200 pounds), an increase of five and a half dimes compared to the previous cheapest price and a decrease of two gold yuan compared to the highest price. According to investigations, the shipping period is April to May, and it is expected that the market will be lively when the goods arrive.

White Zinc Sheets Have Uneven Patterns 217

Recently, the patterns of white zinc sheets in the market have been incomplete. According to investigations, Nos. 3, 4, 7, 9, and 10 are currently lacking in the market. In addition, Nos. 2, 5, 6, and 8, as well as thick patterns, are abundant in circulation. Therefore, the difference between the highest and lowest prices is more than 10 yuan. Currently, the most popular patterns are sold for 134-135 yuan, while the least popular patterns are sold for only about 120 yuan. It is said that only 20 to 30 barrels were sold yesterday.

Finance in the Past Year (Continued 1) 218

— He Boxiong

Shanghai is the commercial center of the country and the main hub for financial allocation. Since the gap between the silver price in Shanghai and the silver price abroad has widened daily, it has been quite profitable to transport silver for export (see the sections on "Foreign Exchange" and "Spot Silver Reserves and Silver Movement" later). Therefore, various foreign merchant banks have been transporting large amounts of silver for export, resulting in a daily tightening of silver in Shanghai. In December of the 23rd year, the highest rate reached six dimes. In January of last year, the interbank lending rate carried on the tight momentum of the previous month and remained firm, with the highest rate being five dimes and five cents. This was because the closing period was near, various industries were replenishing their positions, and there was a demand for funds due to the delivery of public bonds and the year-end cash settlement. Finally, the China, Central, and Communications Banks released 10 million yuan to maintain the market, and the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee also purchased a large amount of spot silver for shipment to Shanghai. By the second half of the month, the situation gradually became peaceful. February was the beginning of the Lunar New Year. Based on past experience, the interbank lending rate in this month should have been extremely low, often referred to as "white paper." However, it opened at two cents at the beginning of the month and suddenly rose to one dime and one cent on the 13th. From the 20th, the foreign market resumed full-day operations, and the situation eased slightly. In March, the interbank lending rate remained at eight to nine cents throughout the month. The financial stagnation was such that the highest rate was nine cents, the lowest was six cents, and the average was eight cents. Adding water to the base rate, except for a rate above one dime at the end of the month, most were also white paper. The situation of apparent ease and hidden tightness had not changed slightly. In early April, the interbank lending market was extremely stable. The interbank lending rate opened at one dime in the early part of the month and gradually increased after the middle part of the month. This was because the long-term loans from "April" were about to expire, and there were not many people actually repaying the loans. Therefore, the interbank lending rate showed an upward trend and reached two dimes by the end of the month. In May, the interbank lending rate, in the first and middle ten days of the month, was stagnant due to the lack of improvement in the commercial market and the financial stagnation. From the 24th, due to the stranding of banks such as Minghua and Meifeng, the base rate soared to as high as three dimes and eight cents. The interbank lending rate ranged from one dime and six cents to one dime and eight cents. The urgency of the situation was no less than that of the Spring Festival in early February and the difficulties at the end of April. June began with the Lunar Dragon Boat Festival and ended with the mid-year closing period, so the finance in this month was particularly tight. In addition, at a time when finance was depleted and panic was rising, the interbank lending rate remained at one dime and eight cents in the first half of the month. In the second half of the month, due to the annual year-end closing of banks and the need to clear transactions between colleagues, the market atmosphere became even more tense, and the interbank lending rate stabilized at two dimes. In July, the interbank lending rate was two dimes throughout the month, except for one dime and eight cents on the 21st. The market atmosphere was exceptionally quiet. In August, the interbank lending rate remained at two dimes in the first and middle ten days of the month, and then gradually decreased in the last ten days, from two dimes to one dime and eight cents, and finally stabilized at one dime and five cents. This was because the financial situation in Shanghai had gradually stabilized in this month, and after the silver and money industry agreed that the China and Communications Banks would stop drawing in, the finance became more and more bland. In September, the interbank lending rate was low, with the average for the whole month being only one dime, three cents and seven mils, a decrease of slightly less than five cents compared to the previous month. The reason for this was that the market gradually stabilized. Even the difficulties of the Mid-Autumn Festival did not show any flaws. In October, the average was one dime and four cents, and the market atmosphere still did not improve. In November, since the reform of the new currency system, the interbank lending rate in the silver and money market in Shanghai has been easing daily. It opened at two dimes at the beginning of the month and had fallen to one dime and two cents by the 15th. Afterwards, it stabilized at one dime and five cents, and then slightly increased at the end of the month. This was because, after the implementation of the new currency system, the issuance of legal tender was more relaxed than before, and the China, Central, and Communications Banks also slightly relaxed their lending to the market. Therefore, the interest rate eased (to be continued).

Women's Special Issue

Married Working Women 219

— Guo Bolin

In recent years, due to economic panic and the difficulty of living, the involvement of married women in the professional front has indeed been a very significant and noteworthy trend. However, on the employer's side, the primary condition for employment is almost always being single, and during layoffs, married women are laid off first. As a result, the insecurity and dissatisfaction of working women are increasing daily.

No matter how you put it, young women with minimal living burdens often lack enthusiasm for their jobs. Even during disputes, although they may be enthusiastic for a while, they cannot permanently maintain their interest in organized movements. However, if the number of people who remain in their positions after marriage continues to increase, women's organizations will become permanent, and their movements will be more active. The foreign example of the heated discussion of the issue of married working women most clearly proves this point.

Last July, the issue was also raised at the Women's Congress of the Belgian Socialist Party held in Brussels, and pregnant women put forward demands that their jobs not be taken away, that they be given special convenience for rest, medical care, or nursing, and that those who have unemployed husbands or unmarried mothers-in-law be regarded as heads of households, and that family allowances be paid to their dependents. Furthermore, women's labor does not threaten men's jobs in any case, and they demonstrate equal or even greater efficiency, but their wages are always lower than men's. They used various facts to prove this and demanded equal pay for equal work. In Belgium, the initial salaries and promotion rates of male and female teachers were originally equal, but they were abolished after the current cabinet was established. However, based on these movements, they were restored last summer.

At the British Labor Party Women's Congress held last June, calls were also made to defend the labor rights of married working women, with equal pay and the protection of the status and health of pregnant women being the focus of the issue.

The layoff of married women is making people with extremely heavy living burdens become victims. And as a result of replacing them with younger, cheaper people, only the wages of women are lowered and their treatment worsened. The defense against this has similarly become the work of the proletariat in various countries.

The Current Situation of Japanese Working Women 220

— Manzhi

Except for Sundays and special holidays, every morning there are groups of young women busily walking to their workplaces. There, machines, paperwork, and all kinds of busy work are waiting for them. Salaries are waiting for them. The rewards of a working life are expanding their freedom. This bright professional life attracts them with one hundred percent of its magic.

Girls who once fantasized about the happiness of married life as a sweet dream lived in the wait to be wives and mothers. Their eyes were only looking inward—toward the family. But now, as soon as they step into real life, their past dreams shatter like bubbles.

Women are constantly advancing on the professional front, and they are experiencing the taste of life in a non-parasitic, independent life. But everyone understands that the professional life of modern women is being developed for the benefit of employers. Even if millions of women are employed, it cannot be considered that the world of women has been opened up and they have entered the door to happiness. For example, the labor conditions in Japan's major industries, silk and textile factories, are criticized as being very bad in the world. The job of selling tickets on buses is very harmful to the female sexual function, and this is often pointed out by general intellectuals. However, the number of women employed is increasing day by day. General banks, companies, stores, etc. are all greatly employing them because women's labor is cheap and can be used cheaply at any time. Not only are married people not dismissed, but there is also a large increase in the number of people who continue to work for a long time, and they have to add a little salary. For example, a telephone operator starts with only eight dimes a day and gradually increases to a monthly salary of forty yuan, fifty yuan, or even eighty yuan, and they are still allowed to continue working.

But in recent years, most of the jobs that women can participate in are mechanical and auxiliary labor that does not require much skill. There is no need for skilled workers who have worked for a long time. Therefore, employers are carrying out a great metabolism, often approaching the work of novices with new interest—new and cheaper workers are what they demand. In this way, in recent years, the issue of the retirement age for working women has been raised.

In Bank A, since the tenth year of Showa, the retirement age for female employees has been reduced from forty-five to thirty years old. In the past, they used to get a raise every year, but now they only get one every other year, and the rate of pay raises has also been reduced to less than two-thirds. Bank B, Bank C, and Company D all have a retirement age of thirty, while Bank E and the bus company even stipulate that the retirement age is twenty-five. (This only applies to clerks and maids, while servants still have a retirement period of twenty years.) Although women are at the height of their working ability at the age of twenty-five or thirty, the ax of retirement is driving them out of the workplace. Women who were welcomed in all workplaces as players in modern industrial society are now being suppressed by the retirement age of thirty.

"Everywhere, I hear people complain. Is this my world?" said Songzi Guanyin to Shan'e.

—

In some places, even if there is no retirement system, they are dismissed because they are married. Even if the matter of marriage is let go, there are many cases where they are dismissed because they are pregnant or giving birth. This is the case in Bank F, Bank G, and Company H. There are also places where "maternity leave" regulations are set, and because there are such regulations that they cannot dismiss married people, they use other methods to dismiss them. Such tragic phenomena can be seen everywhere.

For factory workers, there is legal special protection before and after childbirth. They can receive 60% of their wages during the six-week rest period. In addition, under the application of the Health Insurance Law, they can receive a maternity allowance of 20 yuan. Female teachers also have six weeks of rest before and after childbirth according to the Ministry of Education Order, but the rate of married women in working women is the highest (accounting for 60%), and elementary school teachers who are said to be only competent when married have also had problems because of the resolution made at the Imperial Capital Education Conference in June last year to "grant pregnant female teachers a year of leave." It can be said that the current trend of all working women is like this. In addition to female teachers and female workers, women serving in postal affairs also have regulations for ten weeks of rest before and after childbirth, with 60% of their salary paid, but in general, it has not been implemented. According to newspaper reports, Bank A has a regulation for three weeks of rest during childbirth, but it has not been implemented. The only thing that has been implemented is the practice of being dismissed upon marriage. Even if we take those regulations for three weeks of rest during childbirth, what standards are used to stipulate them? There is really nothing else to say besides using the phrase "better than nothing."

Under these circumstances, the development of women on the professional front has not brought them any happiness. The old illusions have been shattered, but their future is hiding countless reefs.

Russian Working Women Under the Microscope (Part 1) 221

— Zhiyun

"Everyone must work; everyone has a job." This is almost a universal belief in Russia today. Not only the men of the country are like this, but also the women of the country. The completion of the First Five-Year Plan was 42% the responsibility of women. From this, you can see the efforts of Russian women in their work. Indeed, in Russia, almost every woman from the age of sixteen to fifty is a working woman. So in reality, there is no need to add the word "professional" to Russian women.

Russian women have already penetrated into all professional circles. There are traces of women in every profession. These women are the same as men in everything except for their physiological differences. Moreover, there are now some women who have cut their hair short, removed their high heels, and changed into men's clothes, hats, shoes, and socks, completely becoming men. In Moscow, the capital of Russia, an estimated 17% to 20% of women have been altered, and women engaged in heavy industry have the highest heat for alteration, accounting for 40% to 45% of the altered women.

During the First Five-Year Plan, nearly 30% or more of the women in Moscow worked in heavy industry factories. Because the compensation for working in heavy industry factories was more generous than in other professions. However, at that time, the Russian government's management of consumption control was very strict, so although these women received better rewards, their lives were still very difficult. Therefore, at that time, some women, after working six or seven hours a day, asked to continue working for three or four more hours in order to earn a better living wage.

Special Article in this Newspaper

A Record of an Interview with Ms. Zhang Xiangwen 222

— Huang Jiping

Women's professions in China have always been considered very immature. It is already not easy for a woman to succeed in society and gain an economically independent position. If she goes a step further, starts a certain business, and seeks to benefit the public, then she can naturally be considered an outstanding woman. With this thought in mind, I thought of Ms. Zhang Xiangwen. She is a female obstetrician. In the sixth year of the Republic of China, she founded the Renhe Hospital and Obstetrics School on Avenue Joffre. In the eleventh year, she went to the United States to study at the New York Medical Research Institute, and then went to Europe to study various medical careers. With deeper knowledge, she returned to China and developed her ambitions. For the past 20 years, the "Renhe" she has painstakingly managed has been regarded as a complete obstetric hospital at sea. Her spirit and perseverance are admirable. All those who serve in it are women, and most of them are single women. It is no exaggeration to say that "Renhe" is one of the birthplaces of women's professions at sea. This time I had a ten-hour conversation with Ms. Zhang. To sum up, there are the following five points:

"Mrs. Sanger, the leader of the world's birth control movement, has already come to China. People in our country have different views on her. As a famous obstetrician and gynecologist, I wonder what your impressions are of her? I think Mrs. Sanger has attracted people's attention, so I first raised the issue of birth control."

Dr. Zhang answered me without hesitation, as if she had long held her own opinion on this. She said: "Mrs. Sanger's birth control movement is nothing more than arousing people's awareness of the suffering of multiple births and the knowledge of birth control. As for the effect, it may not be significant. Because it is extremely difficult for couples who can reproduce to control themselves or have children on a regular basis. It is by no means something that can be achieved through verbal or written propaganda. Mrs. Sanger has been advocating birth control for many years, but she does not necessarily have effective birth control methods. The medicines and equipment mentioned in ordinary books are not necessarily reliable. Unless women receive practical guidance from doctors, it can be effective."

"I often advise women who have had many children and are too weak to have children to practice birth control, but only 30 to 40 percent of those who can obey the doctor's guidance. It can be seen that birth control methods are not easy to popularize. Couples with nervous diseases, heart disease, lung disease, venereal diseases, etc. are of course not allowed to have children. I advocate that women who have had too many children or are physically weak should practice birth control regardless of whether they are rich or poor. Some people say that the poor should practice birth control, while the rich can have more children. In fact, the children of wealthy families often only know how to spend money and do not engage in proper business, but become social parasites; while the children of poor families are often hardworking and self-motivated, and strive to engage in careers that are beneficial to society and the country. Just look at the history of successful people at home and abroad, ancient and modern, who were born in poverty; but most of the people who do evil are descendants of the declining rich and powerful, so the intellectual class can study eugenics, and birth control is not limited to the rich and poor. I think women can practice birth control after having a maximum of four children. As for women who do not have children, they can only use their energy to serve society. Furthermore, young men and women must not study birth control, otherwise they will inevitably increase invisible dangers. For women who have many children after marriage, there are only two ways to practice birth control: to be pure-hearted and have few desires and to listen to the guidance of doctors." "I heard that Dr. Zhang has always been enthusiastic about social undertakings. May I ask which one you are most interested in in the past?"

"I am very ashamed! I have achieved nothing in the past 20 years, and I have wasted my time. Among the work I have done in the past, I am most interested in Renhe Hospital and the midwifery school. In addition, I have provided financial assistance to those who are suffering and ambitious to pursue advanced studies, subsidized poor students, provided free treatment to poor pregnant women and poor patients, and cultivated talents to serve society. I am satisfied with those who have achieved results. At that time, when I encountered women with serious illnesses and difficult labor, and their lives were in great danger, I was most happy when I treated them and avoided danger. Generally speaking, in the world, everything is most satisfying when extremely difficult difficulties are overcome and success is achieved."

"Dr. Zhang, can you recall the process of founding Renhe Hospital and the midwifery school and how you dealt with the difficulties?"

"I founded Renhe Hospital and the School of Obstetrics and Gynecology in the sixth year of the Republic of China. At that time, there was no school of obstetrics and gynecology in Shanghai, and people did not pay attention to new methods of delivery. Most of the students who enrolled were graduates of middle schools or normal schools, and their level was higher than now. In the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, I bought land to build a house, which is now the address of the hospital on Molier Road. "Renhe" is exactly 20 years old this year. More than 200 midwives have graduated, and they are distributed in various provinces and can serve enthusiastically. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, in order to allow students to practice, I added the Shangxian Hall Women and Children's Hospital and added a nursing school. Speaking of the word difficulty, that is what obstetricians often encounter. For the sake of patients and pregnant women, I often feel restless day and night, and I forget to eat and sleep; I can only sacrifice my own spirit to deal with all the difficulties; fortunately, I am not burdened by family, otherwise I would not be able to bear the busy work."

"What are Dr. Zhang's views on women's professions? And which one is the most suitable?"

"Women's management of household affairs is a basic job. If they can serve society in addition to managing household affairs, then they can be considered outstanding talents. I think women who have economic power often demand specialized academic knowledge: secondly, in addition to ordinary knowledge, they should all learn nursing skills. The old concept of our people often despises nursing, while in European, American and Japanese countries, nurses are very common. Even princesses learn nursing. Because as a nurse, she can serve the family, pay attention to hygiene, or take care of her husband and children, and she will not fail to be a good wife and mother; she can also serve the country, and the front and rear are very important during the war."

"Dr. Zhang is single. May I ask what your views are on the advantages and disadvantages of being single?" I felt a bit awkward before asking the question, but driven by curiosity, I finally raised this overlooked topic.

"I don't advocate women being single, but women who are determined to be single must first have an unbreakable belief, that is, to vow to sacrifice everything of their own and the happiness of their family, and devote themselves to society, only to fulfill their obligations to the public; otherwise, being single will lose its true meaning. In my early years, for the sake of the future of the hospital and the school, I decided to be single, so that my whole body and mind would not be burdened by the family; now, my humble ambition can be considered a small achievement, and I am satisfied. However, I do not hope that others will be single, after all, it also has a great impact on the future of the nation." She said these words with a very serious attitude.

(Recent photo of Ms. Zhang) 223

A Page on Women's Professions in Harbin 224

— Zhu Ga

Now, among the four northeastern provinces, Harbin is the most popular for women's professions. At first, all professions were controlled by men. Since the September 18th Incident, women have slowly found a way out, which is also the beginning of the promotion of women's professions. At that time, various institutions also began to employ female staff. Speaking of women's professions in Harbin, it is really pitiful. Just as a glimmer of dawn appeared in the eyes of the people of Harbin, it disappeared into darkness in the blink of an eye. The kind of women's profession that is污as a "vase" cannot only give women some luck, but instead causes women a lot of pain!

Various institutions completely value appearance over talent when choosing female staff. When applying for a job, they look at the women's heads, bodies, and feet again and again, and then decide whether to stay or leave. If the woman who goes to apply does not have a pretty face, it is difficult to be hired. If hired, they are only given the job of typing, and no other work is given. According to them, "women only have the ability to type." Sometimes, female staff have no work to do, and they have to sit in the office, being browsed and joked. In the beginning, most of these female staff were next to senior staff, and later they became popular in every office, so the incidents of female staff being joked increased even more.

The bosses of the stores have also become smart because of the incident. They know that without female shop assistants to attract customers, the business will not develop, so in order to maintain the economic downturn, they also hire female shop assistants. However, the main condition for the boss to hire female shop assistants is a beautiful face and a slender body. They use the beauty of women to make advertisements and attract customers to come and buy. In less than half a month, the business suddenly developed a lot. At the same time, restaurants also hire female waiters, and opium dens also hire female receptionists. This kind of women's profession seems to be living a hellish life. How can it be said that it is a profession? It is completely a disguised form of selling laughter, exchanging one's flesh and soul for some salary.

Recently, a new type of women's profession has emerged, that is, after the Harbin passenger buses were taken over by the municipal government, the municipal authorities specially recruited a group of female ticket sellers in order to promote women's professions. The requirements were to be young, preferably between the ages of 15 and 25, and to have a senior elementary school education or above. Most of the women who applied were high school graduates. On the first day of the female ticket sellers' work, a group of men scrambled to watch the female ticket sellers. Some even came to ride the bus for a while just to see the female ticket sellers, so the income of the bus that day became an astonishing number. Would anyone be willing to believe that Harbin, known as the "Oriental Little Paris," actually has such a unique phenomenon?

Female Salespersons 225

— Xin

One afternoon, when we opened the back door and thought of strolling on the road, two girls suddenly came. They did not wear any makeup on their faces. Both of them were wearing black cheongsams, and their leather shoes were flat-heeled. Each of them was carrying a small 12-inch leather suitcase.

"Grandma! Do you want to buy some Fragrant Soap?" One of the two saw my wife and came to solicit business; at the same time, she opened her small leather suitcase, which was full of colorful soaps.

"This kind of soap is of very good quality and the price is very cheap. It only sells for eight cents a piece. It is for advertising in our company. You can't buy it anywhere else!" The other continued to babble a lot of words.

Ah! Only then did I realize that they were female salespersons; at the same time, I opened the conversation box and talked with them for a while, and then I understood that the life of female salespersons also has its own pain that others do not know.

Because of the economic downturn in the city, all industries are becoming more and more desolate and declining day by day. Merchants who want to survive this extraordinary period must of course start with sales. Soap is a cosmetic for women. Recruiting a group of girls who have no bread to eat to sell it is really the most appropriate thing to do. The merchants' intentions are not bitter, but the economic downturn is still an economic downturn. If there are no customers for sales, their bread problem still has no solution.

They were originally two of the unemployed. They had only been recruited by a certain company to be female salespersons for two weeks. There was no salary. They would get a rebate of 20 cents for selling one dollar of soap. If there was business, it would not be difficult to earn one or two dollars a month, but in these two weeks, they were running around all day long. As a result, they only sold less than five dollars worth of soap, and the so-called rebate was less than one dollar. Can less than one dollar solve the bread problem for fourteen days?

My wife finally took out 20 cents and 14 copper coins to buy three bars of soap. When they walked out of the alley, I felt that the lives of these two female salespersons were very pitiful!
